class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Single 20-somethings are using AI to start conversations on dating apps because they lack the confidence of older generations, says the boss of Hinge.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Jackie Jantos told the BBC Gen Z daters &quot;absolutely want love&quot; but were &quot;struggling to have the confidence to put themselves out there&quot; as they socialise less in person.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">She defended Hinge&#x27;s AI feature which creates prompts to start chatting with a match as &quot;not about writing words for you&quot; but &quot;helping you express who you are&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Hinge has continued to grow its UK users despite some relationship experts warning of &quot;dating app burnout&quot; and a return to more organic in person meetings.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Founded in 2012 and owned by Match Group, which also owns Tinder and Match.com, Hinge has built its brand around the slogan &quot;designed to be deleted&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Jantos dismisses accusations that this is &quot;just a marketing line&quot;, saying it wants to help users find long-term relationships rather stay on the platform indefinitely.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Tinder is the most visited dating app, but over the past three years usage has been dropping and it&#x27;s now only marginally ahead of nearest competitor Hinge. Bumble and Grindr follow Hinge in the most used dating services. </p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Some 1.5 million adults used Hinge in the year up to May 2025, up from 1.4 million a year earlier.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Over the same period, Tinder&#x27;s audience fell from 1.9 million to 1.5 million, according to Ipsos iris data.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="video-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 hoFfRa"><figure class="sc-cd6075cf-0 laOREU"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 fEqTsi"><div orientation="landscape" class="sc-fcf3f1aa-0"><div class="sc-756ee424-1 dHEzld"><div data-testid="" class="sc-c2960217-0 hTubru"></div><button data-testid="player-play-button" aria-label="Play video" tabindex="0" class="sc-dec3f0fa-1 delfih"><div data-testid="cta-play-icon" class="sc-dec3f0fa-0 arsrU"><svg viewBox="0 0 82 82"><circle cx="41" jsSfKy">Hinge boss on her green and red flags in life</figcaption></div></div></figure></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Speaking to the BBC&#x27;s Big Boss interview podcast, Jantos says Gen Z - who account for more than half of Hinge&#x27;s monthly active users - <a target="_blank" href="https://www.bls.gov/tus/" class="sc-2554282c-0 cDYatN">were spending around 1,000 fewer hours a year in person</a> with other people than those of the same age group two decades ago. </p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Jantos says this equates to more than two hours per day &quot;spent not in the company of another human, but most likely going deep in some sort of experience engaged in your phone&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">She adds: &quot;This prevents people from having the experience of being around others and that is quite a lonely experience.&quot;</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">The 47-year-old says almost half of Gen Z people in the UK now <a target="_blank" href="https://www.oxfam.org.uk/media/press-releases/new-survey-finds-nearly-half-of-gen-z-are-lonely-as-oxfam-encourages-people-to-volunteer/" class="sc-2554282c-0 cDYatN">feel lonely &quot;often or always&quot;.</a> </p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">She says the Covid pandemic meant many young adults missed out on formative years of social interaction.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">&quot;Those years when you&#x27;re sort of experimenting with how you show up in person with another person, how you flirt, how you think about intimacy, that was interrupted for many people,&quot; she says.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="subheadline-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 cJKYng"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 gmICnp"><h2 class="sc-64c6ac20-0 fWTqWp">Dating app burnout</h2></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Dr Carolina Bandinelli, an associate professor at the University of Warwick, who researches dating, relationships and communication agrees that the pandemic changed dating for Gen Z.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">&quot;There was the sense that dating apps are [now] the only way to meet people,&quot; she says. Now she thinks &quot;we are past the hype&quot; as &quot;dating apps didn&#x27;t work as they promised they would&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">She says they were pitched as giving single people &quot;access to a virtually infinite pool of strangers&quot; and sparing them &quot;from the possibility of rejection&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">But &quot;you&#x27;re not really choosing, you&#x27;re more guessing,&quot; she says. &quot;The lack of social cues makes it very difficult.&quot;</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Hinge has an AI tool which users can ask to review their profile and suggest ways to make it more engaging. Another feature offers AI-generated prompts to help users start conversations.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Jantos rejects suggestions that the tools are encouraging people to outsource dating to AI, arguing they are designed to boost confidence rather than replace authentic interactions.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">Siobhan Copland is the founder of Cupid in the City, a matchmaking service for young professionals. She sees many single 20-somethings suffering from dating app burnout.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">&quot;We&#x27;re just constantly bombarded with information...it&#x27;s very much quality connections over quantity [now].&quot;</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">She says the big difference between Gen Z and their predecessors, when it comes to dating, is that &quot;they&#x27;re not really into drinking culture&quot;.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-cd6075cf-0 DQtHs"><div class="sc-82b3c53b-0 IAFLu"><p class="sc-1a18e57c-0 HooNV">&quot;They&#x27;d be more likely at the gym on a Friday night than at the bar,&quot; she says.</p></div></div></div></div><div><div data-component="text-block" class="sc-9cd5bb24-0 lmzibM"><div class="sc-4029fe79-0 hTEgDj">The article&#x27;s headline was amended to reflect Hinge&#x27;s view that their AI feature is an optional tool rather than something Gen Z daters need to use to start
